William Kentridge Biography Selected Works Born Johannesburg, South Africa, 1955 Education University Witwatersrand, Johannesburg, South Africa, 1973-76 Johannesburg Art Foundation, Johannesburg, South Africa, 1976-78 École Jacques LeCoq, Paris, France, 1981-82 Awards Honorary Doctorate, Vrije Universiteit Brussel, 2021 Honorary Doctorate, Faculty of Humanities, University of Pretoria, South Africa, 2018 Penagos Prize, MAPFRE Foundation, 2014 Humanitas Visiting Professor in Contemporary Art at Oxford University, 2013 Distinguished Visiting Humanist at the University of Rochester, New York, 2013 Honorary Doctorate, Royal College of Art, London, 2010 Kyoto Prize, 2010 Honorary Doctorate, Rhodes University, Grahamstown, South Africa, 2008 Honorary Doctorate, University of the Witwatersrand, 2004 Kaiserring Prize, Mönchehaus-Museum für Moderne Kunst, Goslar, Germany, 2003 Sharjah Biennial 6 Prize, United Arab Emirates, April 2003 Residency as Master Artist, Civitella Ranieri Center, Italy, 2000 Carnegie Prize, Carnegie International, Carnegie Museum of Art, Pittsburgh, Pennsylvania, 2000 Hugo Boss Prize (nomination), SoHo Guggenheim, New York, New York, 1998 Standard Bank Young Artist Award, Grahamstown, South Africa, 1987 Weekly Mail Short Film Competition Award, Johannesburg, South Africa for Mine,1991 Weekly Mail Short Film Competition Award, Johannesburg, South Africa for Monument, 1990 Blue Ribbon Award, American Film Festival, New York, New York for Salestalk, 1985 Olive Schreiner Prize for Drama, Cape Town, South Africa for Randlords and Rotgut, (collaboration with Junction Avenue Theatre Company), 1984 Red Ribbon Award for Short Fiction, American Film Festival, New York, New York for Howl at the Moon, 1982 Selected Solo
